# <span data-ttu-id="e1854-104">JavaScript-Versionsinformationen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1854-104">JavaScript version information</span></span>  

[!INCLUDE [deprecation-note](../../includes/legacy-edge-note.md)]  

<span data-ttu-id="e1854-105">Die JavaScript-Unterstützung variiert in Microsoft Edge, Microsoft Store-Apps und unterschiedlichen Dokumentmodi von Internet Explorer \ (IE \).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1854-105">JavaScript support varies across Microsoft Edge, Microsoft Store apps, and different document modes of Internet Explorer \(IE\).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e1854-106">Weitere Informationen zur Versionsverwaltung von IE-Dokumenten Codes finden Sie unter [Definieren der Kompatibilität von Dokumenten](/previous-versions/windows/internet-explorer/ie-developer/compatibility/cc288325(v=vs.85)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1854-106">For more information about IE document code versioning, see [Defining Document Compatibility](/previous-versions/windows/internet-explorer/ie-developer/compatibility/cc288325(v=vs.85)).</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="e1854-107">Die folgende Tabelle enthält eine Zusammenfassung der JavaScript-Unterstützung für Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge und Microsoft Store-Apps.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1854-107">The following table summarizes the JavaScript support across Internet Explorer, Microsoft Edge, and Microsoft Store apps.</span></span>  
  
> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="e1854-108">Experimentelle Funktionen \ (aktiviert von `about:flags` \) sind `Exp.` in einigen Fällen unterscheidet sich der Support für Store-Apps zwischen Windows 8 \ (V8 \) und Windows 10 \ (v10 \)-apps und Windows-Desktop \ (Win \) und Windows Phone \ (Telefon \) wie angegeben.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e1854-108">Experimental features \(enabled from `about:flags`\) are indicated by `Exp.` In some cases, Store apps support varies between Windows 8 \(v8\) and Windows 10 \(v10\) apps, and Windows desktop \(Win\) and Windows Phone \(Phone\), as indicated.</span></span>
